 In such an environment, we are introducing you to the metaphor and terminology associated with war
 1
 Ceasefire- This is a kind of agreement under which two neighboring countries follow the condition of not attacking each other
 yah ek aisa shabd he jo hindustan or pakistan ke sandarbh main sabase adhik sune jane vaala shabd he
 Breaking this agreement is called Ceasefire Violation
 2
 Truce- This term is used for a cease-fire
 Truce ke antargatado yuddhrat deshis nishkarsh par pahunchate hai ki ve tayshuda samay tak kisi bhi prakaar ke hamale nahin karenge
 3
 Firestorm-yah yuddh ke dauraan seemaa ke donon ore hone vaali uthalputhal he
 It is also used for some heavy disputes
 isamen ve kisi baat yaa bindu par ghor asahmat hote hai or yuddh kii sthiti tak pahunch jate hai
 4
 No-man's land-chaahe yuddh kii paristhitiyaan ho yaa phir na ho
 Countries always run under such an agreement that in which areas the army personnel will be stationed and which are not
 ve yathasambhav prayaas karte hai ki ve in samjhauton kaa ulanghan na karen
 5
 Foxhole-is shabd kaa hindi anuwaad to lomadee ke bill ke taur par kiya ja saktaa he
 These are underground pits in which soldiers hide and attack their enemies and protect themselves from all kinds of bombings
 6
 Powder keg- Although it is a small box filled with gunpowder, but in the battlefield, this noun is given to a place or situation which has a strong possibility of becoming non-violent and dangerous
 7
 Dud- Do not confuse this word with the English word Dude
 yud kii shabdaawalee main Dud ko aise shabd ke taur par istemaal karte hai jahaan koi cheez phuss ho jaati he
 Like-all three bombs were duds (ineffectual)
 8
 Surgical Strike- In any confined area, when army takes military action to damage and kill enemies and terrorists, it is called Surgical Strike
 Surgical strikemem is baat kaa dhyaan rakhaa jaataa he ki jis jagah yaa ilaake main aatanki yaa dushman chhipe hue hai sirf usee jagah ko nishaanaa banaaya jaae or isse baaki logon ko koi nuksaan na pahunche

 The center told government departments on Monday that the recruitment process, including advertisement and interview of vacancies, needs to be completed within six months
 rikti ke vigyaapan or pariksha yaa saakshaatkaar kii tithi ke bich lanbaa samay lagane ko dekhte hue yah pahal kii gai he
 The order issued by the Department of Personnel and Training states that this delay can eliminate the opportunity for those candidates who are qualified in the meantime, while creating an atmosphere of uncertainty among the candidates who have applied
 tippaniyan The order said that therefore all ministries or departments are requested to take the initiative to fill the vacant posts through the direct recruitment process, while it can also be ensured that the entire process from advertising to written examination or interview To be finished within six months
 prashasnic mantralayon yaa vibhaagon se kaha gaya he ki unke maatahat swaitshasi nikaayon, lok upkram ke sansthaanon or sanvaidhanik nikaayon ko is tarah kaa nirdesh jari kiya jaae
 The Center has decided that from this year, interviews will not be conducted for recruitment in the categories of Group b (non-gazetted), Group c and Group D
 carmik or prashikshan vibhaag kii taraf se jari aadesh main kaha gaya he, is vilamb se un ummidavaaron ke liye avasar khatm ho saktaa he jo is dauraan yogya hote hai, jabaki jin ummidavaaron ne aavedan kiya he unke bich anischitata kaa maahaul ban jaataa he
 The comments aadesh main kaha gaya ki isliye sabhi mantralayon yaa vibhaagon se anurodh kiya jaataa he ki sidhi bhartee prakriya se khaali padon ko bharne kii pahal kii jaae, vahiin yah bhi sunishchit kiya ja saktaa he ki vigyaapan se lekar likhit pariksha yaa saakshaatkaar karne tak kii puri prakriya chah maheene ke andar khatm kar lee jaae
 Administrative ministries or departments have been asked to issue such directives to autonomous bodies, institutions of public undertakings and constitutional bodies under them
 centre ne nirnay kiya he ki is varsh se samooh bi (gaiyr rajpatrit), samooh si or samooh di kii shreniyon main bhartee ke liye saakshaatkaar nahin liye jaaenge

 iske liye search box main sidhe apane harddisk main seve image ko draig karen
 16) If you are looking for either of two things then use OR between both the words
